================================================================================


FINAL-PLAN
------------------------------
Im missing the concrete action schemas, scenarios, and audit findings. To generate a single coherent PDDL domain and per-scenario problems compatible with FastDownward (STRIPS), please provide the following:

1) Actions and predicates
- Predicates: full list with argument types; note which are static (never deleted).
- Actions: for each action
  - name and parameters (with types)
  - preconditions (including negative ones if any)
  - effects (add/delete), and any derived ordering/phase constraints it must respect
  - any mutual-exclusion or invariants (e.g., resource capacities) that must be encoded as state constraints

2) Types and objects
- Types hierarchy (if any).
- For each scenario: concrete objects per type (no placeholders).

3) Timeline/phase structure (if applicable)
- Discrete phases, days, or time slots; their exact order and contiguity requirements.
- Earliest/exactly/at most timing preferences to be enforced as hard constraints.

4) Audit findings (hard constraints to enforce)
- Prohibited actions or sequences
- Required orderings (must precede/follow), mandatory checkpoints
- Capacity limits, availability windows, exclusivity, segregation-of-duty
- Final state requirements (e.g., final locations, completed tasks that must hold in goal)
- Any avoid/would rather preferences to be treated as strict constraints

5) Scenarios (each becomes a problem file)
For each scenario, specify:
- :objects list (concrete objects)
- :init facts (including static links like adjacency, successor(dayX, dayY), capacities encoded as predicates, etc.)
- :goal facts, fully specifying all mandated terminal conditions
- If costs are required, confirm that action costs are needed; otherwise I will omit :action-costs entirely.

Notes I will follow:
- Requirements limited to :strips, :typing, :negative-preconditions (and :action-costs only if you request costs).
- No placeholder tokens, no penalty/shortfall/quota bookkeeping.
- Ordered sequences and contiguity will be enforced via explicit predicates and goals so plans cannot reorder steps.

Once you share these details (or a structured description I can translate), Ill produce one domain and a separate problem for each scenario, ready for FastDownward.
================================================================================
